id="w-node-e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedaffc-cdedaffa" class="div-block-3"><h2 class="align-center-heading">FAQ</h2><div class="faq-block"><div class="block-grid"><div id="w-node-e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb001-cdedaffa" class="accordian-block"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb002" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">How to Join Discord</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><div class="faq-answer text-block-17 text-block-18"><a href="https://discord.gg/gorillatag" target="_blank" class="faq-link">Join our Discord!</a><a href="#" class="hide"><br></a>Discord is currently our <strong>ONLY</strong> official channel.&nbsp; News for the game is posted in the #announcements channel.<br><br>Please review and pay close attention to the #rules.</div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb015" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb016" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">Code Of Conduct</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><div class="faq-answer">- NO RACISM, SEXISM, HOMOPHOBIA, TRANSPHOBIA, OR OTHER FORMS&nbsp;OF&nbsp;BIGOTRY.<br><br>- NO CHEATS OR MODS.<br><br>- DO NOT HARASS OTHER PLAYERS OR INTENTIONALLY MAKE THEM UNCOMFORTABLE.<br><br>- DO NOT TROLL OR GRIEF LOBBIES BY BEING UNCATCHABLE OR BY ESCAPING THE MAP. TRY TO MAKE SURE EVERYONE IS HAVING FUN.<br><br>-IF SOMEONE IS BREAKING THIS CODE, PLEASE REPORT THEM.<br><br>- PLEASE BE NICE GORILLAS AND HAVE A GOOD TIME!</div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb02d" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb02e" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">Room and Player Names</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><div class="faq-answer">Players are given a one-time warning if the room or player name that they have entered into the computer will trigger a ban.<br><br>If a player sees this warning - They should not repeat the same name or any other ban-worthy name.<br><br>Do not use a Room or Lobby name unless confident that it will not result in a ban.</div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb03c" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb03d" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">Managing Playspace Best Practices</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">Muting</h3><div class="faq-answer">Players can mute other players from the big board in-game.&nbsp; There is a mute button that can be toggled.&nbsp; The mute setting persists between sessions and is stored locally.&nbsp; The setting needs to be re-enabled if the game is uninstalled from the device.<br><br>To mute all players, Voice comms can be disabled from the in-game computer.<br><strong><strong></strong></strong></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">Reporting</h3><div class="faq-answer">In-game, players can report other players that are not following the Code of Conduct at the big board. Please report any player that is not following the Code - Every report helps flag players that need to be reviewed for a ban-worthy offense.<br><br>You must be a member of the Discord channel to access the form. Players can be reported outside of the game with this form:<br><br><a href="https://dyno.gg/form/8fd71b14" target="_blank" class="faq-link">REPORTING&nbsp;FORM</a><br></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">BAns</h3><div class="faq-answer">We hold our Code of Conduct and treat bans seriously.&nbsp; If a player is determined to not be following the rules, we will issue bans aggressively with escalating time durations.<br><br>Some things to note:<br>1. Players will be given a specific reason for a ban on the red message board.&nbsp; When submitting an appeal, please reference the <em>exact</em> wording on the board so the Appeals team knows exactly which ban to look up.<br>2. Ganging up on a player and spam or mass reporting them does not affect our decision making process.&nbsp; We consider context when reviewing reports and look out for that behavior specifically.<br>3. Many Bans are issued for patterns of behavior.&nbsp; If an appeal is for a specific incident, the player’s past behavior and prior ban history are considered.<br>4. Any report with evidence or a trusted witness is more likely to be acted upon.<br><strong><strong></strong></strong></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">IP&nbsp;Bans</h3><div class="faq-answer">If a player's ban escalations have reached a point where we ban an IP address, all users from that IP address are subject to a ban.&nbsp; A player may trigger a ban evasion if we determine that they have:<br><br>1. Reinstalled the app to attempt to manipulate time.<br>2. Used a different account on the headset.<br>3. Used a Steam account when they were banned on Quest (or vice-versa)<br><br>If a player receives an IP ban, they should not attempt to login to the servers with any device, or any other account.&nbsp; This will be considered Ban Evasion and an additional ban will be added after the current ban expires.&nbsp; It does not matter if a player owns this account or if they have other members of their household attempting to login with their own accounts.&nbsp; When in this situation, we suggest players discuss their&nbsp; behavior with the other members of their household and educate them on following the Code of Conduct.<br><br>IP Bans can stack.&nbsp; If a banned player continues to attempt to evade the IP ban, additional bans will be added.&nbsp; These may appear as if players are immediately banned after the current ban timer expires.<br><br>In extreme cases, we will issue a permanent ban.&nbsp; The red board will notify players if they have received a permanent ban.&nbsp; Their only recourse is to make an appeal.<br><strong><strong></strong></strong></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">Appeals</h3><div class="faq-answer">A ban appeal can be made by visiting our<br>‍<br><a href="https://dyno.gg/form/5265c968" target="_blank" class="faq-link">BAN&nbsp;APPEAL&nbsp;FORM</a><br>and filling it out by typing "/appeal" and following the prompts from the public channel on the Discord.<br><br>Appeals are handled by the Appeals Team.&nbsp; This team is intentionally separate from any of the Gorilla Tag team that have day-to-day interactions with customers.&nbsp; Developers, Community Moderators, Volunteer Moderators, Stick or Twigs do not participate in the review process.&nbsp; Do not contact them about appeals or additional restrictions may be applied.<br><br>Players must provide accurate information in their appeal.&nbsp; If the Appeals Team is unable to locate their account because of incorrect information, the appeal will be denied.<br></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">DIscord Bans &amp;&nbsp;Appeals</h3><div class="faq-answer">To appeal a Discord Ban.&nbsp; Please visit the following link and fill out the form.<br><br><a href="https://dyno.gg/form/975514e0" target="_blank" class="faq-link"><strong class="faq-link">DISCORD&nbsp;BAN&nbsp;APPEAL&nbsp;FORM</strong></a></div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0a9" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0aa" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">Opting in to Beta and How to Change Release Channels</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><h3 class="faq-subheading">On Steam</h3><div class="faq-answer">Go to the setting for Gorilla Tag on Steam and select <em>Properties &gt; Beta</em> and from the drop down select the desired beta channel.<br><br><a href="https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/883121484137132032/1017448198052270162/optin_to_beta.gif" target="_blank" class="faq-link">VIDEO</a><br></div><h3 class="faq-subheading">On Quest</h3><div class="faq-answer"><a href="https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/883121484137132032/1017448198052270162/optin_to_beta.gif" target="_blank"></a>In a browser, visit the Gorilla Tag product page at: <br>‍<a href="https://www.oculus.com/experiences/quest/4979055762136823/" target="_blank" class="faq-link">PRODUCT&nbsp;PAGE</a><br>Under the “Additional Details” section, select the desired version next to the <em>Version</em> row.<br><br><a href="https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/883121484137132032/1017448166804705340/SVID_20210411_172330_1.mp4" target="_blank" class="faq-link">VIDEO</a><br>Switching back to Live:<br>To switch back to the Live published version of the game, follow the steps above except select the “Live” version of the game.&nbsp; You may need to uninstall and reinstall to force the update on your device.<br></div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0d4" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0d5" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">When I start the game, the board shows <strong>0 Players online</strong></div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><div class="faq-answer"><em>PC</em>: Reboot your Router if that doesn't work. Remove all mods and try again.<br><br>‍<em>Quest</em>: This may be the new Meta Account update. Visit this link to update.<br><br><a href="https://auth.meta.com/" target="_blank" class="faq-link">META&nbsp;UPDATE<br></a><br>Create your account, ensure your headset is fully charged and go to Settings &gt; Software update &gt; and click the Check for updates. Let the device update and follow instructions on the headset. You may need to restart your headset<br></div></div></div><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0ef" class="accordian-item" style="transform: translate3d(0px, 50px, 0px) scale3d(1, 1, 1) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) rotateZ(0deg) skew(0deg, 0deg); transform-style: preserve-3d; opacity: 0;"><div data-w-id="e688c257-b66a-6985-ab2a-0f41cdedb0f0" class="faq-q"><div class="plus-icon"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636837e648a569adae070150_faq-arrow-up.svg" loading="lazy" alt=""></div><div class="faq-heading-regular">Accepting the Terms of Service and Privacy Policy</div></div><div class="faq-ans" style="height: 0px;"><div class="faq-answer">Users will be prompted to accept the Terms of Service and/or Privacy Policy at game startup every time Another Axiom has modified those agreements.<br><br>To accept each agreement, <strong>HOLD</strong> a Face button (A, B, X, or Y on your controller) to acknowledge that the user has read, understood, and agrees to the terms of the agreements.</div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><section class="footer-light"><div class="container-2"><div class="footer-wrapper-two"><a id="w-node-_05f365df-c542-0170-2b82-9c2b777daf7f-777daf7c" href="/" aria-current="page" class="footer-brand w-inline-block w--current"><img src="https://uploads-ssl.webflow.com/634dcd98720fb26a457ae36f/636e8c5ef118dfbec481f11d_Cropped-Wordmark-White.svg" loading="lazy" width="Auto" height="150" alt="cropped gorilla tag vr logo
